<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toga.html>toga</a> (18335)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:toga.html>toga</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toga.html>toga</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toga.html>toga</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:s.html>s</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toga.html>togaatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

***toko.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toko.html>toko</a> (24027)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> Indonesian <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms"><a href = vnd.unilang:toko.html>toko</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:shop.html>shop</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_Min" class="extiw" title="w:Southern Min"><a href = vnd.unilang:min.html>Min</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nan.html>Nan</a></a></span> <span class="Hani" lang="zh">土庫</span>／<span class="Hani" lang="zh">土库</span> (<i><span class="tr Latn">thó͘-khò͘</span></i>, “private storehouse”).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
